介观·杭州Hangzhou 2026
MoCA Weland — Lhasa, Xizang

介·观

介而观之 — 当代艺术博物馆Weland — Museum of Contemporary Art
SCROLL
Origin · 溯源Origin

从From拉萨河畔the Banks of the Lhasa River
生长的艺术场域A Growing Art Field

介观——介而观之。这个建筑缘起于一个藏区孩子的私心，想为西藏留下一片对于藏区文化的具象理解。七岁第一次进藏，十二岁离开，三十一岁再回西藏，二十多年的时间里，— Weland. This building originated from a Tibetan child's wish to preserve a tangible understanding of Tibetan culture. First entering Tibet at seven, leaving at twelve, returning at thirty-one — over twenty years,介观便也孕育而生了。Weland was born.

十六年前在拉萨河畔一片联排别墅走入了我的眼中。建筑整体延续藏式收分（下大上小）的审美语言，以「保留—介入—整合」为原则，将原有建筑群整合为「T」形构图。Sixteen years ago, a row of townhouses on the banks of the Lhasa River caught my eye. The architecture follows the Tibetan tapering aesthetic, reshaping the buildings into a "T"-shaped composition under the principle of "preserve — intervene — integrate."

介观的肌理源自西藏的花岗岩、灵芝的松木和藏地的红铜。11 位工匠历时一年半手工锻造的铜料，随时间氧化变色，夯土与白色涂层的结合，使建筑成为「生长的有机体」。The textures draw from Tibetan granite, Linzhi pine, and Tibetan copper. Copper hand-forged by 11 craftsmen over eighteen months oxidizes with time. The combination of rammed earth and white coating makes the building a "growing organism."

2020意大利 A' Design AwardItaly A' Design Award
空间设计类铜奖Bronze Award in Spatial Design
2023爱普生数字光影系统Epson Digital Light System
《1/84000》装置Installations计划Program
Multifunctional · 多维场域Multifunctional · Multi-dimensional Field

一个空间，无数One Space, Infinite可能Possibilities

介观不仅是美术馆——艺术活动、展陈装置与生活空间在统一建筑语境中实现多生态共存。Weland is not merely a museum — art events, exhibition installations, and living spaces coexist within a unified architectural context.

不染Unstained
BURAN · THE UNSTAINED
高达 9 米的钢板剪影，取自艺术家韩书力同名作品。它是A 9-meter-tall steel silhouette inspired by artist Han Shuli's work. It is介观的精神核心，「更换佛衣」已成为延续至今的展览仪式。2023 年起搭载爱普生数字光影系统，佛衣成为动态流动的视觉语言。the spiritual core. "Changing the Buddha's Robe" has become an ongoing ritual. Since 2023, with the Epson digital light system, the robe has become a dynamic visual language.
桥Bridge
BRIDGE
将城市廊Bringing the urban corridor桥Bridge结构引入室内，由等距排列的细长矩形铜柱构成立面秩序，同时解决了两排别墅间连廊的扶手与安全问题。建筑即structure indoors — evenly spaced slender copper columns form façade order while solving handrail and safety issues. Architecture is装置Installations，装置Installations即建筑。is architecture.
水坛城 · 金字塔Water Mandala · Pyramid
WATER MANDALA
圆形玻璃穹顶以纯铜包裹，构成向天敞开的天井，引入自然光，赋予空间精神指向。其灵感源于哥特与拜占庭建筑中的穹顶构型，表达向上、仰望的精神内核。A circular glass dome wrapped in pure copper opens skyward, introducing natural light. Inspired by Gothic and Byzantine domes, it expresses the spiritual essence of reaching upward.

介观·杭州Hangzhou

Mesoscopic · Hangzhou — 2026 Autumn

Hangzhou · 链接之地Hangzhou · Land of Connection

从拉萨到From Lhasa to良渚Liangzhu
跨越山河的能量链接An Energy Link Across Mountains and Rivers

西藏Tibet介观落地arriving in杭州Hangzhou良渚，并非简单的地理位移，而是一场跨越山河的能量链接。这里不是终途，而是连接雪域精神与江南气韵的创造性场域。Liangzhu is not a geographic relocation, but an energy link across mountains and rivers — a creative field connecting the spirit of the snowy plateau with the elegance of Jiangnan.

位于良渚古城遗址公园旁的观山LAND，四栋建筑共 1,602㎡——展厅、藏式Bistro、艺术家驻地工作室、精品住宿、修身疗愈空间、户外草坪，以活动系统串联不同建筑体及公共空间。Located beside Liangzhu Ancient City Park, Guanshan LAND comprises four buildings totaling 1,602㎡ — exhibition halls, Tibetan Bistro, artist studios, boutique accommodation, wellness spaces, and outdoor lawns.

介观·杭州Hangzhou所传达的是一种世界观——精髓不在于「中间点」，而在于「连接处」所迸发的张力与创造力。What Weland conveys is a worldview — the essence lies not in the "midpoint," but in the tension and creativity at the "connection."

Programs · 项目Projects

思想Idea发生器Generator

将静态空间转化为动态的思想发生器。以活动系统串联不同建筑体及公共空间，链接并活化孤立的单体。Transforming static spaces into dynamic idea generators — connecting buildings and public spaces, activating isolated units.

🎨
展览 · 策展Exhibition · Curation
Exhibition & Curation
藏地艺术节、Tibetan Art Festival, 古物藏毯展Ancient Tibetan Carpet Exhibition、布面重彩联展Heavy Color on Canvas Exhibition、冈仁波齐国际展。分布式展览贯穿四栋建筑与户外草坪。, Mount Kailash International Exhibition. Distributed exhibitions span all buildings and lawns.
🎵
演出 · 音疗Performance · Sound Healing
Performance & Sound Healing
喜马拉雅专题音乐演出、藏地颂钵音疗会、AV展演。通高主展厅与户外草坪双场地联动。Himalayan music performances, Tibetan singing bowl sessions, AV exhibitions. Double-height hall and lawn dual-venue coordination.
🖌
驻地 · 创作Residency · Creation
Artist Residency
三个独立工作室接纳青年艺术家入驻创作。「第三极」艺文Three independent studios welcome young artists. "Third Pole" Arts项目Projects，联动拉萨母馆与阳朔糖舍。, linking the Lhasa main museum and Yangshuo Sugar House.
🧘
修身 · 疗愈Wellness · Healing
Healing & Meditation
集体冥想、瑜伽课程、辟谷体验、藏药课程。在良渚 5000 年古老土地上开辟精神栖居之所。Meditation, yoga, fasting, Tibetan medicine classes — a spiritual dwelling on Liangzhu's 5,000-year-old ancient land.
🍵
藏食 · 藏咖Tibetan Cuisine · Coffee
Tibetan Bistro & Café
藏式Bistro餐厅、窑炉面包房、藏咖啡与藏茶。10.3m 长吧台，藏地买手店与Tibetan Bistro, kiln bakery, Tibetan coffee and tea. 10.3m bar counter, Tibetan select shop and介观氆氇产品系列。pulu textile line.
🏕
过林卡 · 市集Lingka · Market
Lingka & Market
藏地「林卡」文化的当代演绎。草坪市集、露营、Contemporary Tibetan "Lingka" culture. Lawn markets, camping,介观氆氇秀场。四季不同的活动在此轮番上演。pulu fashion shows. Seasonal activities take turns here.

2026 Autumn — A Place of Link

介观 WELAND

介观当代艺术博物馆致力于西藏传统与当代艺术的收藏、研究和展示，以公益性、艺术性、教育性丰富人们的文化生活。Weland MoCA is dedicated to the collection, research, and exhibition of Tibetan traditional and contemporary art.
